# <a name="msmq-queue-class"></a><span data-ttu-id="1de88-107">MSMQ-Queue 類別</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1de88-107">MSMQ-Queue class</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="1de88-108">MSMQ 使用者會根據其需求，建立 MMC 或 MSMQ API)  (的佇列。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1de88-108">MSMQ users create queues (by MMC or by MSMQ API) according to their requirements.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="1de88-109">佇列會與特定電腦相關聯，並放在該電腦的 MSMQ-Configuration 下。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1de88-109">A queue is associated with a specific computer, and is placed under the MSMQ-Configuration of that computer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="1de88-110">每一部電腦的佇列數目沒有任何限制。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1de88-110">There is no limit to the number of queues per computer.</span></span>
